Hello, List!
Here are the listings as of May 07, 2014.


Listings Project Story of the Week:
I just wanted to share my story with you. I was in a terrible bind as to my living situation in March and had to move. And while I had a lovely place to &quot;crash&quot;, I really wanted a home. The Wednesday before I was supposed to move I received the listing project email. I said to myself &quot;If nothing's perfect, I'll just go ahead with my crash plans&quot;. Well, I found it! I am paying below market for a fabulous space in a great neighborhood with lovely roommates. Your listings project was a game changer for me. I can't thank you enough! -Ruby


Best,
Stephanie
